The ranking of the cards in this deck are as follows (from high to low); Ace, King, Queen, Jack, 10, 9, 8, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2. \r\n\r\nThe player who draws the highest card of all would be designated the first dealer. \r\n\r\nThe dealer shuffles the cards and deals the hand. If no trump card has been played to the trick, the highest card of the suit led wins the trick. The winner of each trick leads the first card to the next trick. Each captured trick should be kept in a face down pile of cards, gathered by the winner of the trick. \r\n\r\nAfter all 13 tricks have been played the captured cards are then examined to determine the winner of the hand. \r\n\r\nIf one partnership manages to capture three or four of the Tens, they win the hand.
